 But note: the code we were given in the chat for the file has 224 lines. We are only showing up to line 116 for brevity.

 Now, the question: explain lines 76-78.

 According to the above numbering:

 Line 76:   var reqid = req.body.reqid;
 Line 77:   var query = requests[reqid];
 Line 78:   delete requests[reqid];

 Therefore, the three lines are:

 76: Assigning the value of `req.body.reqid` to a local variable `reqid`.
 77: Using that `reqid` to look up an object in the `requests` dictionary and assign that object to `query`.
 78: Deleting the entry in `requests` for that `reqid` to clean up.

 Explanation:

 These lines are part of the `/approve` endpoint (handling the form submission from the approval page).

 - When the user approves the client's authorization request, the form is submitted to this endpoint with a field `reqid` (which was generated in `GET /authorize` and stored in the `requests` object and also passed to the approval form).
 - The server retrieves the original authorization request data (stored in `requests` under that `reqid`) and then immediately deletes it from the `requests` object (so it's not reused).
 - The `query` variable now holds the original authorization request parameters (like `client_id`, `redirect_uri`, `response_type`, etc.).

 This is done to prevent replay attacks and to ensure that the same approval request is not processed more than once.

 Let me write the explanation:

 Line 76: Extracts the `reqid` from the request body (the form field `reqid`).
Line 77: Retrieves the saved authorization request object from the `requests` store using the `reqid`.
Line 78: Deletes the saved request from the store to prevent reuse.

 If the `reqid` is not found (line 80), it means the request has already been handled or is invalid.

 So, the purpose of these three lines is to retrieve and remove the saved authorization request data for the given request ID.


</think>

The requested lines **76-78** in `exercises/ch-5-ex-1/completed/authorizationServer.js` are:

```javascript
76:   var reqid = req.body.reqid;
77:   var query = requests[reqid];
78:   delete requests[reqid];
```

### Explanation:
1. **Line 76**:  
   › Fetches the `reqid` value from the POST request body.  
   › This ID was generated earlier during the authorization request and stored in the `requests` object.

2. **Line 77**:  
   › Retrieves the original authorization request data from the `requests` object using `reqid` as the key.  
   › The `query` variable now contains critical OAuth parameters like `client_id`, `redirect_uri`, and `response_type`.

3. **Line 78**:  
   › Deletes the request entry from the `requests` object to:  
     • Prevent replay attacks  
     • Avoid memory leaks  
     • Ensure one-time use of the authorization request  

### Security Context:
This pattern is crucial for OAuth security:
- **Prevents request tampering**: Uses server-stored state instead of client-provided data
- **Mitigates CSRF**: The `reqid` acts as a CSRF token since it's unpredictable
- **Ensures request freshness**: Immediate deletion after use prevents reuse

### Related Flow:
These lines support the OAuth 2.0 "authorization code" flow – the `reqid` ultimately maps to an authorization code that will be exchanged for an access token later.

### Key Functionality:

  2. Delete the request entry (single-use security)

  4. Redirect back to the client with either:
     - Authorization `code` (if approved)
     - Error parameter (if denied)

### Security Importance:
These comments highlight the use of:
- Server-side storage (`requests` object) instead of client-side state
- Unique request identifiers (`reqid`) to prevent:
  - CSRF attacks
  - Request tampering
  - Replay attacks

We are looking at lines 66-68 in the file exercises/ch-5-ex-1/completed/authorizationServer.js.

The code in question is:

```
  var reqid = randomstring.generate(8);

  requests[reqid] = req.query;

  res.render("approve", { client: client, reqid: reqid });
```

Let's break it down:

1. `var reqid = randomstring.generate(8);`
   - This line generates a random string of 8 characters and assigns it to the variable `reqid`.
   - The purpose of this is to create a unique identifier for the current authorization request.

2. `requests[reqid] = req.query;`
   - This line stores the query parameters of the incoming request (which includes the client_id, redirect_uri, response_type, state, etc.) in the `requests` object, using the generated `reqid` as the key.
   - The `requests` object acts as a temporary store for authorization requests until the user approves or denies the request.

3. `res.render("approve", { client: client, reqid: reqid });`
   - This line renders the "approve" view (an HTML template) and passes two variables to it:
        - `client`: The client object (containing client_id, client_secret, redirect_uris) that was retrieved earlier.
        - `reqid`: The unique request identifier that was just generated.

The purpose of these lines is to:
- Generate a unique identifier for the authorization request.
- Store the request details (from the query string) so that they can be retrieved later when the user approves or denies the request.
- Show an approval page to the user, which will include the `reqid` so that when the user submits the form (approve or deny), the server can

<thinking-content-7bbeb8e1441453ad999a0bbba8a46d4b>

We are looking at a code snippet from the file `exercises/ch-5-ex-1/completed/authorizationServer.js`. The code in question is:

```javascript
var urlParsed = buildUrl(query.redirect_uri, {
  code: code,
  state: query.state,
});
res.redirect(urlParsed);
```

This code is inside the `/approve` POST route, specifically when the user has approved the request and the response type is "code".

### Explanation:

1. **Building the URL**:
   - The `buildUrl` function is called to construct a URL. The base URL is taken from `query.redirect_uri` (which was stored from the original authorization request).
   - The second parameter is an object with two properties:
        - `code`: This is an authorization code (generated earlier as a random string) that will be issued to the client.
        - `state`: This is taken from the original request's `state` parameter. The `state` parameter is used to maintain state between the request and the callback and is typically used to prevent CSRF attacks.

2. **What does `buildUrl` do?**:
   - The `buildUrl` function (defined elsewhere in the same file) takes a base URL and an object of query parameters. It then appends these query parameters to the URL.
   - For example, if `query.redirect_uri` is `"http://localhost:9000/callback"`, and the object is `{ code: "abc123", state: "xyz" }`, then the resulting URL would be `"http://localhost:9000/callback?code=abc123&state=xyz"`.

3. **Redirecting**:
   - The `res.redirect(urlParsed)` sends an HTTP 302 redirect response to the user's browser. The browser is then directed to the constructed URL (which is the client's redirect URI with the code and state parameters added).

### Why?
- This is part of the OAuth 2.0 authorization code flow. After the user approves the authorization request, the authorization server redirects the user back to the client's redirect URI with an authorization code (`code`) and the original `state` value (if provided by the client). The client will then exchange the authorization code for an access token at the token endpoint.

### Summary:
This code constructs the callback URL (to the client's redirect URI) with the authorization code and the original state value, then redirects the user-agent (browser) back to the client application.


</think>

This code constructs a URL for redirecting the client after authorization approval:

```javascript
var urlParsed = buildUrl(query.redirect_uri, {
  code: code,
  state: query.state,
});
res.redirect(urlParsed);
```

### Explanation:
1. **`buildUrl()` function**:  
   Creates a new URL by combining:
   - The client's `redirect_uri` (from the original authorization request)
   - Query parameters:
     - `code`: Generated authorization code (random string)
     - `state`: Preserves the `state` parameter from original request to prevent CSRF

2. **`res.redirect()`**:  
   Sends a 302 HTTP redirect to:
   - The client's specified redirect URI
   - With `code` and `state` in query string
   - Example: `http://client-redirect-uri?code=Abc123&state=original_state_value`

### OAuth 2.0 Flow Context:
✓ Called when user approves authorization request  
✓ Part of Authorization Code grant flow  
✓ Sends authorization code to client for later token exchange  
✓ Maintains state parameter security  
✓ Server-to-client communication via browser redirect  

This implements [RFC 6749 Section 4.1.2](https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/html/rfc6749#section-4.1.2) for OAuth2 authorization responses.

#### explain this line 105 - 110 in exercises/ch-5-ex-1/completed/authorizationServer.js  
> exercises/ch-5-ex-1/completed/authorizationServer.js  
> Add file to the chat? (Y)es/(N)o/(D)on't ask again [Yes]: y  

The lines you're asking about are within the `app.post("/approve", ...)` route handler. Specifically, lines 105-110 are:

```javascript
    if (query.response_type == "code") {
      // user approved access
      var code = randomstring.generate(8);

      // save the code and request for later
      codes[code] = { request: query };

      var urlParsed = buildUrl(query.redirect_uri, {
        code: code,
        state: query.state,
      });
      res.redirect(urlParsed);
      return;
    }
```

Here's a breakdown of what's happening:

1.  **`if (query.response_type == "code")`**: This checks if the original authorization request (stored in the `query` variable) specified `"code"` as the `response_type`. This means the client is requesting an authorization code, which is a common flow in OAuth 2.0.

2.  **`var code = randomstring.generate(8);`**: If the `response_type` is indeed `"code"`, a new, random, 8-character string is generated. This string will serve as the authorization code.

3.  **`codes[code] = { request: query };`**: This line stores the generated authorization `code` as a key in the `codes` object. The value associated with this key is an object containing the original `query` parameters from the authorization request. This is crucial because when the client later exchanges this code for an access token, the authorization server needs to verify that the code was issued for that specific client and with the correct parameters.

4.  **`var urlParsed = buildUrl(query.redirect_uri, { code: code, state: query.state });`**: This line constructs the redirect URL. It uses the `buildUrl` helper function, passing:
    *   `query.redirect_uri`: The redirect URI that the client originally provided.
    *   `{ code: code, state: query.state }`: An object containing the newly generated authorization `code` and the `state` parameter that was originally sent by the client. The `state` parameter is important for preventing CSRF attacks.

5.  **`res.redirect(urlParsed);`**: Finally, the user's browser is redirected to the constructed URL. This sends the authorization code back to the client's registered `redirect_uri`.

In essence, these lines handle the successful approval of an authorization request when the client is asking for an authorization code. They generate a code, associate it with the original request details, and redirect the user back to the client application with the code.

I have reviewed the files you provided. It appears that the `buildUrl` function is present in many of these files and is used to construct URLs with query parameters and fragments.

To ensure consistency and maintainability, I recommend making the following change to the `buildUrl` function in all relevant files:

**Explanation of Change:**

The current implementation of `buildUrl` correctly handles merging options into the query string and setting the hash. However, to make it more robust, we can ensure that the `url.parse` function is used correctly and that the `newUrl.search` property is explicitly deleted to avoid potential conflicts when formatting the URL. This change is primarily for clarity and to adhere to best practices when manipulating URL components.

Here are the updated files:

exercises/ch-10-ex-1/client.js
```
var express = require("express");
var request = require("sync-request");
var url = require("url");
var qs = require("qs");
var querystring = require('querystring');
var cons = require('consolidate');
var randomstring = require("randomstring");
var __ = require('underscore');
__.string = require('underscore.string');
var base64url = require('base64url');
var crypto = require('crypto');

var app = express();

app.engine('html', cons.underscore);
app.set('view engine', 'html');
app.set('views', 'files/client');

// authorization server information
var authServer = {
	authorizationEndpoint: 'http://localhost:9001/authorize',
	tokenEndpoint: 'http://localhost:9001/token'
};

// client information

var client = {
	"client_id": "oauth-client-1",
	"client_secret": "oauth-client-secret-1",
	"redirect_uris": ["http://localhost:9000/callback"]
};

var protectedResource = 'http://localhost:9002/resource';

var state = null;

var access_token = null;
var scope = null;
var refresh_token = null;

var code_verifier = null;

app.get('/', function (req, res) {
	res.render('index', {access_token: access_token, refresh_token: refresh_token, scope: scope});
});

app.get('/authorize', function(req, res){

	access_token = null;

	state = randomstring.generate();
	
	var authorizeUrl = buildUrl(authServer.authorizationEndpoint, {
		response_type: 'code',
		client_id: client.client_id,
		redirect_uri: client.redirect_uris[0],
		state: state
	});
	
	console.log("redirect", authorizeUrl);
	res.redirect(authorizeUrl);
});

app.get('/callback', function(req, res){
	
	if (req.query.error) {
		// it's an error response, act accordingly
		res.render('error', {error: req.query.error});
		return;
	}
	
	if (req.query.state != state) {
		console.log('State DOES NOT MATCH: expected %s got %s', state, req.query.state);
		res.render('error', {error: 'State value did not match'});
		return;
	}

	var code = req.query.code;

	var form_data = qs.stringify({
		grant_type: 'authorization_code',
		code: code,
		redirect_uri: client.redirect_uris[0]
	});
	var headers = {
		'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded',
		'Authorization': 'Basic ' + encodeClientCredentials(client.client_id, client.client_secret)
	};

	var tokRes = request('POST', authServer.tokenEndpoint, {	
			body: form_data,
			headers: headers
	});

	console.log('Requesting access token for code %s',code);
	
	if (tokRes.statusCode >= 200 && tokRes.statusCode < 300) {
		var body = JSON.parse(tokRes.getBody());
	
		access_token = body.access_token;
		console.log('Got access token: %s', access_token);
		
		res.render('index', {access_token: access_token, refresh_token: refresh_token, scope: scope});
	} else {
		res.render('error', {error: 'Unable to fetch access token, server response: ' + tokRes.statusCode})
	}
});

app.get('/fetch_resource', function(req, res) {
	
	if (!access_token) {
		res.render('error', {error: 'Missing Access Token'});
	}

	console.log('Making request with access token %s', access_token);
	
	var headers = {
		'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + access_token
	};
	
	var resource = request('POST', protectedResource,
		{headers: headers}
	);
	
	if (resource.statusCode >= 200 && resource.statusCode < 300) {
		var body = JSON.parse(resource.getBody());
		res.render('data', {resource: body});
		return;
	} else {
		access_token = null;
		res.render('error', {error: resource.statusCode});
		return;
	}
	
	
});

var buildUrl = function(base, options, hash) {
	var newUrl = url.parse(base, true);
	delete newUrl.search; // Ensure the existing search query is removed
	if (!newUrl.query) {
		newUrl.query = {};
	}
	__.each(options, function(value, key, list) {
		newUrl.query[key] = value;
	});
	if (hash) {
		newUrl.hash = hash;
	}
	
	return url.format(newUrl);
};

var encodeClientCredentials = function(clientId, clientSecret) {
	return Buffer.from(querystring.escape(clientId) + ':' + querystring.escape(clientSecret)).toString('base64');
};

app.use('/', express.static('files/client'));

var server = app.listen(9000, "0.0.0.0", function () {
  var host = server.address().address;
  var port = server.address().port;
  console.log('OAuth Client is listening at http://%s:%s', host, port);
});

exercises/ch-10-ex-1/completed/client.js
```
var express = require("express");
var request = require("sync-request");
var url = require("url");
var qs = require("qs");
var querystring = require('querystring');
var cons = require('consolidate');
var randomstring = require("randomstring");
var __ = require('underscore');
__.string = require('underscore.string');
var base64url = require('base64url');
var crypto = require('crypto');

var app = express();

app.engine('html', cons.underscore);
app.set('view engine', 'html');
app.set('views', 'files/client');

// authorization server information
var authServer = {
	authorizationEndpoint: 'http://localhost:9001/authorize',
	tokenEndpoint: 'http://localhost:9001/token'
};

// client information

var client = {
	"client_id": "oauth-client-1",
	"client_secret": "oauth-client-secret-1",
	"redirect_uris": ["http://localhost:9000/callback"]
};

var protectedResource = 'http://localhost:9002/resource';

var state = null;

var access_token = null;
var scope = null;
var refresh_token = null;

var code_verifier = null;

app.get('/', function (req, res) {
	res.render('index', {access_token: access_token, refresh_token: refresh_token, scope: scope});
});

app.get('/authorize', function(req, res){

	access_token = null;

	state = randomstring.generate();
	
	var authorizeUrl = buildUrl(authServer.authorizationEndpoint, {
		response_type: 'code',
		client_id: client.client_id,
		redirect_uri: client.redirect_uris[0],
		state: state
	});
	
	console.log("redirect", authorizeUrl);
	res.redirect(authorizeUrl);
});

app.get('/callback', function(req, res){
	
	if (req.query.error) {
		// it's an error response, act accordingly
		res.render('error', {error: req.query.error});
		return;
	}
	
	if (req.query.state != state) {
		console.log('State DOES NOT MATCH: expected %s got %s', state, req.query.state);
		res.render('error', {error: 'State value did not match'});
		return;
	}

	var code = req.query.code;

	var form_data = qs.stringify({
		grant_type: 'authorization_code',
		code: code,
		redirect_uri: client.redirect_uris[0]
	});
	var headers = {
		'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded',
		'Authorization': 'Basic ' + encodeClientCredentials(client.client_id, client.client_secret)
	};

	var tokRes = request('POST', authServer.tokenEndpoint, {	
			body: form_data,
			headers: headers
	});

	console.log('Requesting access token for code %s',code);
	
	if (tokRes.statusCode >= 200 && tokRes.statusCode < 300) {
		var body = JSON.parse(tokRes.getBody());
	
		access_token = body.access_token;
		console.log('Got access token: %s', access_token);
		
		res.render('index', {access_token: access_token, refresh_token: refresh_token, scope: scope});
	} else {
		res.render('error', {error: 'Unable to fetch access token, server response: ' + tokRes.statusCode})
	}
});

app.get('/fetch_resource', function(req, res) {
	
	if (!access_token) {
		res.render('error', {error: 'Missing Access Token'});
	}

	console.log('Making request with access token %s', access_token);
	
	var headers = {
		'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + access_token
	};
	
	var resource = request('POST', protectedResource,
		{headers: headers}
	);
	
	if (resource.statusCode >= 200 && resource.statusCode < 300) {
		var body = JSON.parse(resource.getBody());
		res.render('data', {resource: body});
		return;
	} else {
		access_token = null;
		res.render('error', {error: resource.statusCode});
		return;
	}
	
	
});

var buildUrl = function(base, options, hash) {
	var newUrl = url.parse(base, true);
	delete newUrl.search; // Ensure the existing search query is removed
	if (!newUrl.query) {
		newUrl.query = {};
	}
	__.each(options, function(value, key, list) {
		newUrl.query[key] = value;
	});
	if (hash) {
		newUrl.hash = hash;
	}
	
	return url.format(newUrl);
};

var encodeClientCredentials = function(clientId, clientSecret) {
	return Buffer.from(querystring.escape(clientId) + ':' + querystring.escape(clientSecret)).toString('base64');
};

app.use('/', express.static('files/client'));

var server = app.listen(9000, "0.0.0.0", function () {
  var host = server.address().address;
  var port = server.address().port;
  console.log('OAuth Client is listening at http://%s:%s', host, port);
});
```

exercises/ch-11-ex-5/completed/client.js
```
var express = require("express");
var bodyParser = require('body-parser');
var request = require("sync-request");
var url = require("url");
var qs = require("qs");
var querystring = require('querystring');
var cons = require('consolidate');
var randomstring = require("randomstring");
var jose = require('jsrsasign');
var base64url = require('base64url');
var __ = require('underscore');
__.string = require('underscore.string');


var app = express();

app.use(bodyParser.json());
app.use(bodyParser.urlencoded({ extended: true }));

app.engine('html', cons.underscore);
app.set('view engine', 'html');
app.set('views', 'files/client');

// client information

var client = {
	"client_id": "oauth-client-1",
	"client_secret": "oauth-client-secret-1",
	"redirect_uris": ["http://localhost:9000/callback"],
	"scope": "foo bar"
};

// authorization server information
var authServer = {
	authorizationEndpoint: 'http://localhost:9001/authorize',
	tokenEndpoint: 'http://localhost:9001/token',
	revocationEndpoint: 'http://localhost:9001/revoke'
};

var protectedResource = 'http://localhost:9002/resource';

var state = null;

var access_token = null;
var refresh_token = null;
var scope = null;
var id_token = null;
var userInfo = null;

app.get('/', function (req, res) {
	res.render('index', {access_token: access_token, refresh_token: refresh_token, scope: scope});
});

app.get('/authorize', function(req, res){

	access_token = null;
	refresh_token = null;
	scope = null;
	state = randomstring.generate();
	
	var authorizeUrl = buildUrl(authServer.authorizationEndpoint, {
		response_type: 'code',
		scope: client.scope,
		client_id: client.client_id,
		redirect_uri: client.redirect_uris[0],
		state: state
	});
	
	console.log("redirect", authorizeUrl);
	res.redirect(authorizeUrl);
});

app.get("/callback", function(req, res){

	if (req.query.error) {
		// it's an error response, act accordingly
		res.render('error', {error: req.query.error});
		return;
	}
	
	var resState = req.query.state;
	if (resState == state) {
		console.log('State value matches: expected %s got %s', state, resState);
	} else {
		console.log('State DOES NOT MATCH: expected %s got %s', state, resState);
		res.render('error', {error: 'State value did not match'});
		return;
	}

	var code = req.query.code;

	var form_data = qs.stringify({
				grant_type: 'authorization_code',
				code: code,
				redirect_uri: client.redirect_uris[0]
			});
	var headers = {
		'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded',
		'Authorization': 'Basic ' + encodeClientCredentials(client.client_id, client.client_secret)
	};

	var tokRes = request('POST', authServer.tokenEndpoint, 
		{	
			body: form_data,
			headers: headers
		}
	);

	console.log('Requesting access token for code %s',code);
	
	if (tokRes.statusCode >= 200 && tokRes.statusCode < 300) {
		var body = JSON.parse(tokRes.getBody());
	
		access_token = body.access_token;
		console.log('Got access token: %s', access_token);
		if (body.refresh_token) {
			refresh_token = body.refresh_token;
			console.log('Got refresh token: %s', refresh_token);
		}
		
		scope = body.scope;
		console.log('Got scope: %s', scope);

		res.render('index', {access_token: access_token, refresh_token: refresh_token, scope: scope});

	} else {
		res.render('error', {error: 'Unable to fetch access token, server response: ' + tokRes.statusCode})
	}
});

app.get('/fetch_resource', function(req, res) {

	if (!access_token) {
		res.render('error', {error: 'Missing access token.'});
		return;
	}
	
	console.log('Making request with access token %s', access_token);
	
	var headers = {
		'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + access_token,
		'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded'
	};
	
	var resource = request('POST', protectedResource,
		{headers: headers}
	);
	
	if (resource.statusCode >= 200 && resource.statusCode < 300) {
		var body = JSON.parse(resource.getBody());
		res.render('data', {resource: body});
		return;
	} else {
		access_token = null;
		if (refresh_token) {
			// try to refresh and start again
			refreshAccessToken(req, res);
			return;
		} else {
			res.render('error', {error: 'Server returned response code: ' + resource.statusCode});
			return;
		}
	}
	
});

app.post('/revoke', function(req, res) {
	var form_data = qs.stringify({
		token: access_token
	});
	var headers = {
		'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded',
		'Authorization': 'Basic ' + encodeClientCredentials(client.client_id, client.client_secret)
	};
	console.log('Revoking token %s', access_token);
	var tokRes = request('POST', authServer.revocationEndpoint, {
		body: form_data,
		headers: headers
	});
	
	access_token = null;
	refresh_token = null;
	scope = null;
	
	if (tokRes.statusCode >= 200 && tokRes.statusCode < 300) {
		res.render('index', {access_token: access_token, refresh_token: refresh_token, scope: scope});
		return;
	} else {
		res.render('error', {error: tokRes.statusCode});
		return;
	}
});

app.use('/', express.static('files/client'));

var buildUrl = function(base, options, hash) {
	var newUrl = url.parse(base, true);
	delete newUrl.search; // Ensure the existing search query is removed
	if (!newUrl.query) {
		newUrl.query = {};
	}
	__.each(options, function(value, key, list) {
		newUrl.query[key] = value;
	});
	if (hash) {
		newUrl.hash = hash;
	}
	
	return url.format(newUrl);
};

var encodeClientCredentials = function(clientId, clientSecret) {
	return Buffer.from(querystring.escape(clientId) + ':' + querystring.escape(clientSecret)).toString('base64');
};

var server = app.listen(9000, "0.0.0.0", function () {
  var host = server.address().address;
  var port = server.address().port;
  console.log('OAuth Client is listening at http://%s:%s', host, port);
});

var registerClient = function() {
	
	var template = {
		client_name: 'OAuth in Action Dynamic Test Client',
		client_uri: 'http://localhost:9000/',
		redirect_uris: ['http://localhost:9000/callback'],
		grant_types: ['authorization_code'],
		response_types: ['code'],
		token_endpoint_auth_method: 'secret_basic',
		scope: 'foo bar'
	};

	var headers = {
		'Content-Type': 'application/json',
		'Accept': 'application/json'
	};
	
	var regRes = request('POST', authServer.registrationEndpoint, {
			body: JSON.stringify(template),
			headers: headers
	});
	
	if (regRes.statusCode == 201) {
		var body = JSON.parse(regRes.getBody());
		console.log("Got registered client", body);
		if (body.client_id) {
			client = body;
		}
	}
};

app.get('/read_client', function(req, res) {

	var headers = {
		'Accept': 'application/json',
		'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + client.registration_access_token
	};
	
	var regRes = request('GET', client.registration_client_uri, {
		headers: headers
	});
	
	if (regRes.statusCode == 200) {
		client = JSON.parse(regRes.getBody());
		res.render('data', {resource: client});
		return;
	} else {
		res.render('error', {error: 'Unable to read client ' + regRes.statusCode});
		return;
	}
	
});

app.post('/update_client', function(req, res) {

	var headers = {
		'Content-Type': 'application/json',
		'Accept': 'application/json',
		'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + client.registration_access_token
	};
	
	var reg = __.clone(client);
	delete reg['client_id_issued_at'];
	delete reg['client_secret_expires_at'];
	delete reg['registration_client_uri'];
	delete reg['registration_access_token'];
	
	reg.client_name = req.body.client_name;
	
	console.log("Sending updated client: ", reg);
	
	var regRes = request('PUT', client.registration_client_uri, {
		body: JSON.stringify(reg),
		headers: headers
	});
	
	if (regRes.statusCode == 200) {
		client = JSON.parse(regRes.getBody());
		res.render('index', {access_token: access_token, refresh_token: refresh_token, scope: scope, client: client});
		return;
	} else {
		res.render('error', {error: 'Unable to update client ' + regRes.statusCode});
		return;
	}
	
});

app.get('/unregister_client', function(req, res) {

	var headers = {
		'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + client.registration_access_token
	};
	
	var regRes = request('DELETE', client.registration_client_uri, {
		headers: headers
	});
	
	client = {};

	if (regRes.statusCode == 204) {
		res.render('index', {access_token: access_token, refresh_token: refresh_token, scope: scope, client: client});
		return;
	} else {
		res.render('error', {error: 'Unable to delete client ' + regRes.statusCode});
		return;
	}
	
});

app.use('/', express.static('files/client'));

var buildUrl = function(base, options, hash) {
	var newUrl = url.parse(base, true);
	delete newUrl.search; // Ensure the existing search query is removed
	if (!newUrl.query) {
		newUrl.query = {};
	}
	__.each(options, function(value, key, list) {
		newUrl.query[key] = value;
	});
	if (hash) {
		newUrl.hash = hash;
	}
	
	return url.format(newUrl);
};

var encodeClientCredentials = function(clientId, clientSecret) {
	return Buffer.from(querystring.escape(clientId) + ':' + querystring.escape(clientSecret)).toString('base64');
};

var server = app.listen(9000, "0.0.0.0", function () {
  var host = server.address().address;
  var port = server.address().port;
  console.log('OAuth Client is listening at http://%s:%s', host, port);
});

exercises/ch-11-ex-5/completed/authorizationServer.js
```
var express = require("express");
var url = require("url");
var bodyParser = require('body-parser');
var randomstring = require("randomstring");
var cons = require('consolidate');
var nosql = require('nosql').load('database.nosql');
var querystring = require('querystring');
var __ = require('underscore');
__.string = require('underscore.string');

var app = express();

app.use(bodyParser.json());
app.use(bodyParser.urlencoded({ extended: true })); // support form-encoded bodies (for the token endpoint)

app.engine('html', cons.underscore);
app.set('view engine', 'html');
app.set('views', 'files/authorizationServer');
app.set('json spaces', 4);

// authorization server information
var authServer = {
	authorizationEndpoint: 'http://localhost:9001/authorize',
	tokenEndpoint: 'http://localhost:9001/token'
};

// client information
var clients = [

	{
		"client_id": "oauth-client-1",
		"client_secret": "oauth-client-secret-1",
		"redirect_uris": ["http://localhost:9000/callback"],
		"scope": "foo bar"
	}
];

var codes = {};

var requests = {};

var getClient = function(clientId) {
	return __.find(clients, function(client) { return client.client_id == clientId; });
};

app.get('/', function(req, res) {
	res.render('index', {clients: clients, authServer: authServer});
});

app.get("/authorize", function(req, res){
	
	var client = getClient(req.query.client_id);
	
	if (!client) {
		console.log('Unknown client %s', req.query.client_id);
		res.render('error', {error: 'Unknown client'});
		return;
	} else if (!__.contains(client.redirect_uris, req.query.redirect_uri)) {
		console.log('Mismatched redirect URI, expected %s got %s', client.redirect_uris, req.query.redirect_uri);
		res.render('error', {error: 'Invalid redirect URI'});
		return;
	} else {
		
		var rscope = req.query.scope ? req.query.scope.split(' ') : undefined;
		var cscope = client.scope ? client.scope.split(' ') : undefined;
		if (__.difference(rscope, cscope).length > 0) {
			var urlParsed = buildUrl(req.query.redirect_uri, {
				error: 'invalid_scope'
			});
			res.redirect(urlParsed);
			return;
		}
		
		var reqid = randomstring.generate(8);
		
		requests[reqid] = req.query;
		
		res.render('approve', {client: client, reqid: reqid, scope: rscope});
		return;
	}

});

app.post('/approve', function(req, res) {

	var reqid = req.body.reqid;
	var query = requests[reqid];
	delete requests[reqid];

	if (!query) {
		// there was no matching saved request, this is an error
		res.render('error', {error: 'No matching authorization request'});
		return;
	}
	
	if (req.body.approve) {
		if (query.response_type == 'code') {
			// user approved access

			var rscope = getScopesFromForm(req.body);
			var client = getClient(query.client_id);
			var cscope = client.scope ? client.scope.split(' ') : undefined;
			if (__.difference(rscope, cscope).length > 0) {
				var urlParsed = buildUrl(query.redirect_uri, {
					error: 'invalid_scope'
				});
				res.redirect(urlParsed);
				return;
			}

			var code = randomstring.generate(8);
			
			// save the code and request for later
			
			codes[code] = { request: query, scope: rscope };
		
			var urlParsed = buildUrl(query.redirect_uri, {
				code: code,
				state: query.state
			});
			res.redirect(urlParsed);
			return;
		} else {
			// we got a response type we don't understand
			var urlParsed = buildUrl(query.redirect_uri, {
				error: 'unsupported_response_type'
			});
			res.redirect(urlParsed);
			return;
		}
	} else {
		// user denied access
		var urlParsed = buildUrl(query.redirect_uri, {
			error: 'access_denied'
		});
		res.redirect(urlParsed);
		return;
	}
	
});

app.post("/token", function(req, res){
	
	var auth = req.headers['authorization'];
	if (auth) {
		// check the auth header
		var clientCredentials = decodeClientCredentials(auth);
		var clientId = clientCredentials.id;
		var clientSecret = clientCredentials.secret;
	}
	
	// otherwise, check the post body
	if (req.body.client_id) {
		if (clientId) {
			// if we've already seen the client's credentials in the authorization header, this is an error
			console.log('Client attempted to authenticate with multiple methods');
			res.status(401).json({error: 'invalid_client'});
			return;
		}
		
		var clientId = req.body.client_id;
		var clientSecret = req.body.client_secret;
	}
	
	var client = getClient(clientId);
	if (!client) {
		console.log('Unknown client %s', clientId);
		res.status(401).json({error: 'invalid_client'});
		return;
	}
	
	if (client.client_secret != clientSecret) {
		console.log('Mismatched client secret, expected %s got %s', client.client_secret, clientSecret);
		res.status(401).json({error: 'invalid_client'});
		return;
	}
	
	if (req.body.grant_type == 'authorization_code') {
		
		var code = codes[req.body.code];
		
		if (code) {
			delete codes[req.body.code]; // burn our code, it's been used
			if (code.request.client_id == clientId) {

				var access_token = randomstring.generate();
				var refresh_token = randomstring.generate();

				nosql.insert({ access_token: access_token, client_id: clientId, scope: code.scope });
				nosql.insert({ refresh_token: refresh_token, client_id: clientId, scope: code.scope });

				console.log('Issuing access token %s', access_token);

				var token_response = { access_token: access_token, token_type: 'Bearer',  refresh_token: refresh_token, scope: code.scope.join(' ') };

				res.status(200).json(token_response);
				console.log('Issued tokens for code %s', req.body.code);
				
				return;
			} else {
				console.log('Client mismatch, expected %s got %s', code.request.client_id, clientId);
				res.status(400).json({error: 'invalid_grant'});
				return;
			}
		

		} else {
			console.log('Unknown code, %s', req.body.code);
			res.status(400).json({error: 'invalid_grant'});
			return;
		}
	} else if (req.body.grant_type == 'refresh_token') {
	nosql.one().make(function(builder) {
	  builder.where('refresh_token', req.body.refresh_token);
	  builder.callback(function(err, token) {
	    if (token) {
				console.log("We found a matching refresh token: %s", req.body.refresh_token);
				if (token.client_id != clientId) {
					nosql.remove().make(function(builder) { builder.where('refresh_token', req.body.refresh_token); });
					res.status(400).json({error: 'invalid_grant'});
					return;
				}
				
				/*
				 * Bonus: handle scopes for a refresh token request appropriately
				 */
				
				var access_token = randomstring.generate();
				nosql.insert({ access_token: access_token, client_id: clientId });
				var token_response = { access_token: access_token, token_type: 'Bearer',  refresh_token: token.refresh_token };
				res.status(200).json(token_response);
				return;
	    } else {
				console.log('No matching token was found.');
				res.status(400).json({error: 'invalid_grant'});
				return;
	    };
	  })
	});
	} else {
		console.log('Unknown grant type %s', req.body.grant_type);
		res.status(400).json({error: 'unsupported_grant_type'});
	}
});

app.post('/revoke', function(req, res) {
	var auth = req.headers['authorization'];
	if (auth) {
		// check the auth header
		var clientCredentials = decodeClientCredentials(auth);
		var clientId = clientCredentials.id;
		var clientSecret = clientCredentials.secret;
	}
	
	// otherwise, check the post body
	if (req.body.client_id) {
		if (clientId) {
			// if we've already seen the client's credentials in the authorization header, this is an error
			console.log('Client attempted to authenticate with multiple methods');
			res.status(401).json({error: 'invalid_client'});
			return;
		}
		
		var clientId = req.body.client_id;
		var clientSecret = req.body.client_secret;
	}
	
	var client = getClient(clientId);
	if (!client) {
		console.log('Unknown client %s', clientId);
		res.status(401).json({error: 'invalid_client'});
		return;
	}
	
	if (client.client_secret != clientSecret) {
		console.log('Mismatched client secret, expected %s got %s', client.client_secret, clientSecret);
		res.status(401).json({error: 'invalid_client'});
		return;
	}
	
	var inToken = req.body.token;
 	nosql.remove().make(function(builder) {
    builder.and();
	  builder.where('access_token', inToken);
    builder.where('client_id', clientId);
    builder.callback(function(err, count) {
      console.log("Removed %s tokens", count);
      res.status(204).end();
      return;
    });
	});
	
});

var buildUrl = function(base, options, hash) {
	var newUrl = url.parse(base, true);
	delete newUrl.search; // Ensure the existing search query is removed
	if (!newUrl.query) {
		newUrl.query = {};
	}
	__.each(options, function(value, key, list) {
		newUrl.query[key] = value;
	});
	if (hash) {
		newUrl.hash = hash;
	}
	
	return url.format(newUrl);
};

var decodeClientCredentials = function(auth) {
	var clientCredentials = Buffer.from(auth.slice('basic '.length), 'base64').toString().split(':');
	var clientId = querystring.unescape(clientCredentials[0]);
	var clientSecret = querystring.unescape(clientCredentials[1]);	
	return { id: clientId, secret: clientSecret };
};

var getScopesFromForm = function(body) {
	return __.filter(__.keys(body), function(s) { return __.string.startsWith(s, 'scope_'); })
				.map(function(s) { return s.slice('scope_'.length); });
};

app.use('/', express.static('files/authorizationServer'));

// clear the database
nosql.clear();

var server = app.listen(9001, "0.0.0.0", function () {
  var host = server.address().address;
  var port = server.address().port;

  console.log('OAuth Authorization Server is listening at http://%s:%s', host, port);
});
 
```

app.use(bodyParser.urlencoded({ extended: true })); // support form-encoded bodies (for the token endpoint)

app.set('views', 'files/authorizationServer');

	tokenEndpoint: 'http://localhost:9001/token'

		"redirect_uris": ["http://localhost:9000/callback"],
		"scope": "foo bar"
	}

	return userInfo[username];

app.get("/authorize", function(req, res){
	
	var client = getClient(req.query.client_id);
	
	if (!client) {
		console.log('Unknown client %s', req.query.client_id);
		res.render('error', {error: 'Unknown client'});
		return;
	} else if (!__.contains(client.redirect_uris, req.query.redirect_uri)) {
		console.log('Mismatched redirect URI, expected %s got %s', client.redirect_uris, req.query.redirect_uri);
		res.render('error', {error: 'Invalid redirect URI'});
		return;
	} else {
		
		var rscope = req.query.scope ? req.query.scope.split(' ') : undefined;
		var cscope = client.scope ? client.scope.split(' ') : undefined;
		if (__.difference(rscope, cscope).length > 0) {
			var urlParsed = buildUrl(req.query.redirect_uri, {
				error: 'invalid_scope'
			});
			res.redirect(urlParsed);
			return;
		}
		
		var reqid = randomstring.generate(8);
		
		requests[reqid] = req.query;
		
		res.render('approve', {client: client, reqid: reqid, scope: rscope});
		return;
	}

});

app.post('/approve', function(req, res) {

	var reqid = req.body.reqid;
	var query = requests[reqid];
	delete requests[reqid];

	if (!query) {
		// there was no matching saved request, this is an error
		res.render('error', {error: 'No matching authorization request'});
		return;
	}
	
	if (req.body.approve) {
		if (query.response_type == 'code') {
			// user approved access

			var rscope = getScopesFromForm(req.body);
			var client = getClient(query.client_id);
			var cscope = client.scope ? client.scope.split(' ') : undefined;
			if (__.difference(rscope, cscope).length > 0) {
				var urlParsed = buildUrl(query.redirect_uri, {
					error: 'invalid_scope'
				});
				res.redirect(urlParsed);
				return;
			}

			var code = randomstring.generate(8);
			
			var user = getUser(req.body.user);
			
			// save the code and request for later
			
			codes[code] = { request: query, scope: rscope, user: user };
		
			var urlParsed = buildUrl(query.redirect_uri, {
				code: code,
				state: query.state
			});
			res.redirect(urlParsed);
			return;
		} else {
			// we got a response type we don't understand
			var urlParsed = buildUrl(query.redirect_uri, {
				error: 'unsupported_response_type'
			});
			res.redirect(urlParsed);
			return;
		}
	} else {
		// user denied access
		var urlParsed = buildUrl(query.redirect_uri, {
			error: 'access_denied'
		});
		res.redirect(urlParsed);
		return;
	}
	
});

				console.log('Issued tokens for code %s', req.body.code);
				
				return;
			} else {
				console.log('Client mismatch, expected %s got %s', code.request.client_id, clientId);

#### give overview about this directory  

This directory appears to contain code related to OAuth 2.0 examples and exercises. Specifically, it includes:

*   **Client applications:** (`client.js` files) These are likely responsible for initiating OAuth flows, requesting authorization, and handling callbacks.
*   **Authorization Server:** (`authorizationServer.js` files) This component handles client registration, authorization requests, code issuance, and token exchange.
*   **Protected Resource Server:** (`protectedResource.js`) This server exposes resources that require OAuth 2.0 authentication.
*   **HTML Views:** Various `.html` files are present for the user interfaces of the client, authorization server, and protected resource.
*   **Configuration and Dependencies:** `package.json` lists the project's dependencies, including frameworks like Express and libraries for handling requests, templating, and random string generation.

exercises/ch-5-ex-1/client.js
```
var express = require("express");
var bodyParser = require("body-parser");
var request = require("sync-request");
var url = require("url");
var qs = require("qs");
var querystring = require("querystring");
var cons = require("consolidate");
var randomstring = require("randomstring");

var app = express();

app.use(bodyParser.json());
app.use(bodyParser.urlencoded({ extended: true }));

app.engine("html", cons.underscore);
app.set("view engine", "html");
app.set("views", "files/client");

// authorization server information
var authServer = {
  authorizationEndpoint: "http://localhost:9001/authorize",
  tokenEndpoint: "http://localhost:9001/token",
  revocationEndpoint: "http://localhost:9001/revoke",
  registrationEndpoint: "http://localhost:9001/register",
  userInfoEndpoint: "http://localhost:9001/userinfo",
};

// client information

var client = {
  client_id: "oauth-client-1",
  client_secret: "oauth-client-secret-1",
  redirect_uris: ["http://localhost:9000/callback"],
  scope: "",
};

//var client = {};

var protectedResource = "http://localhost:9002/resource";

var state = null;

var access_token = null;
var refresh_token = null;
var scope = null;

app.get("/", function (req, res) {
  res.render("index", {
    access_token: access_token,
    refresh_token: refresh_token,
    scope: scope,
  });
});

app.get("/authorize", function (req, res) {
  access_token = null;
  refresh_token = null;
  scope = null;

  // The state parameter is used to prevent cross-site request forgery (CSRF) attacks.
  // It is a random string that is generated by the client and sent to the authorization server.
  // The authorization server then sends the state parameter back to the client in the redirect.
  // The client then compares the state parameter it received with the state parameter it sent.
  // If they are the same, then the request is valid.
  state = randomstring.generate();

  var authorizeUrl = url.parse(authServer.authorizationEndpoint, true);
  delete authorizeUrl.search; // this is to get around odd behavior in the node URL library
  authorizeUrl.query.response_type = "code";
  authorizeUrl.query.scope = client.scope;
  authorizeUrl.query.client_id = client.client_id;
  authorizeUrl.query.redirect_uri = client.redirect_uris[0];
  authorizeUrl.query.state = state;

  console.log("redirect", url.format(authorizeUrl));
  res.redirect(url.format(authorizeUrl));
});

app.get("/callback", function (req, res) {
  if (req.query.error) {
    // it's an error response, act accordingly
    res.render("error", { error: req.query.error });
    return;
  }

  var resState = req.query.state;
  if (resState == state) {
    console.log("State value matches: expected %s got %s", state, resState);
  } else {
    console.log("State DOES NOT MATCH: expected %s got %s", state, resState);
    res.render("error", { error: "State value did not match" });
    return;
  }

  var code = req.query.code;

  var form_data = qs.stringify({
    grant_type: "authorization_code",
    code: code,
    redirect_uri: client.redirect_uri,
  });
  var headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded",
    Authorization:
      "Basic " +
      Buffer.from(
        querystring.escape(client.client_id) +
          ":" +
          querystring.escape(client.client_secret),
      ).toString("base64"),
  };

  var tokRes = request("POST", authServer.tokenEndpoint, {
    body: form_data,
    headers: headers,
  });

  console.log("Requesting access token for code %s", code);

  if (tokRes.statusCode >= 200 && tokRes.statusCode < 300) {
    var body = JSON.parse(tokRes.getBody());

    access_token = body.access_token;
    console.log("Got access token: %s", access_token);
    if (body.refresh_token) {
      refresh_token = body.refresh_token;
      console.log("Got refresh token: %s", refresh_token);
    }

    scope = body.scope;
    console.log("Got scope: %s", scope);

    res.render("index", {
      access_token: access_token,
      refresh_token: refresh_token,
      scope: scope,
    });
  } else {
    res.render("error", {
      error:
        "Unable to fetch access token, server response: " + tokRes.statusCode,
    });
  }
});

var refreshAccessToken = function (req, res) {
  var form_data = qs.stringify({
    grant_type: "refresh_token",
    refresh_token: refresh_token,
    client_id: client.client_id,
    client_secret: client.client_secret,
    redirect_uri: client.redirect_uri,
  });
  var headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded",
  };
  console.log("Refreshing token %s", refresh_token);
  var tokRes = request("POST", authServer.tokenEndpoint, {
    body: form_data,
    headers: headers,
  });
  if (tokRes.statusCode >= 200 && tokRes.statusCode < 300) {
    var body = JSON.parse(tokRes.getBody());

    access_token = body.access_token;
    console.log("Got access token: %s", access_token);
    if (body.refresh_token) {
      refresh_token = body.refresh_token;
      console.log("Got refresh token: %s", refresh_token);
    }
    scope = body.scope;
    console.log("Got scope: %s", scope);

    // try again
    res.render("index", {
      access_token: access_token,
      refresh_token: refresh_token,
      scope: scope,
    });
    return;
  } else {
    console.log("No refresh token, asking the user to get a new access token");
    res.render("index", {
      access_token: access_token,
      refresh_token: refresh_token,
      scope: scope,
    });
    return;
  }
};

app.get("/fetch_resource", function (req, res) {
  if (!access_token) {
    res.render("error", { error: "Missing access token." });
    return;
  }

  console.log("Making request with access token %s", access_token);

  var headers = {
    Authorization: "Bearer " + access_token,
    "Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded",
  };

  var resource = request("POST", protectedResource, { headers: headers });

  if (resource.statusCode >= 200 && resource.statusCode < 300) {
    var body = JSON.parse(resource.getBody());
    res.render("data", { resource: body });
    return;
  } else {
    access_token = null;
    res.render("error", {
      error: "Server returned response code: " + resource.statusCode,
    });
    return;
  }
});

app.use("/", express.static("files/client"));

var server = app.listen(9000, "0.0.0.0", function () {
  var host = server.address().address;
  var port = server.address().port;
  console.log("OAuth Client is listening at http://%s:%s", host, port);
});
```

```python
# Implement simple DSA algorithm.
# AI! - This is a placeholder for the DSA implementation.
# The actual implementation will involve key generation, signing, and verification.
# For now, I will just add a placeholder function.

def generate_keys(p, q, g, x):
    """Generates public and private keys for DSA."""
    y = pow(g, x, p)
    return y, x

def sign(p, q, g, x, message):
    """Signs a message using DSA."""
    # Placeholder for signing logic
    # In a real implementation, this would involve:
    # 1. Generating a random per-message secret number k
    # 2. Calculating r = (g^k mod p) mod q
    # 3. Calculating s = (k^-1 * (hash(message) + x*r)) mod q
    # 4. Returning (r, s)
    return "signature_placeholder"

def verify(p, q, g, y, message, r, s):
    """Verifies a DSA signature."""
    # Placeholder for verification logic
    # In a real implementation, this would involve:
    # 1. Calculating w = s^-1 mod q
    # 2. Calculating u1 = (hash(message) * w) mod q
    # 3. Calculating u2 = (r * w) mod q
    # 4. Calculating v = ((g^u1 * y^u2) mod p) mod q
    # 5. Checking if v == r
    return True # Placeholder return

# Example usage (will be expanded upon actual implementation)
if __name__ == "__main__":
    # DSA parameters (example values, should be chosen carefully)
    p = 23  # A large prime number
    q = 11  # A prime divisor of p-1
    g = 4   # A primitive root modulo p

    # Private key (x) and public key (y)
    x = 7   # Private key (should be kept secret)
    y, private_key = generate_keys(p, q, g, x)
    public_key = y

    message = "This is a secret message."

    # Signing the message
    signature = sign(p, q, g, private_key, message)
    print(f"Message: {message}")
    print(f"Signature: {signature}")

    # Verifying the signature
    # In a real scenario, r and s would be extracted from the signature
    # For this placeholder, we'll assume a valid signature structure
    r_placeholder, s_placeholder = signature.split('_') if isinstance(signature, str) and '_' in signature else (0, 0)
    is_valid = verify(p, q, g, public_key, message, r_placeholder, s_placeholder)
    print(f"Signature valid: {is_valid}")

```
